{% block scripts %}
<script>
// ===== タブ切り替え =====
function switchMainTab(name, btn) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.main-tab-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.main-tab-content').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('active'));
  document.getElementById('tab-' + name).classList.add('active');
  btn.classList.add('active');
  // URLハッシュ対応
  history.replaceState(null, '', '#tab-' + name);
}

function switchSubTab(name, btn) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.sub-tab-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.sub-tab-content').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('active'));
  document.getElementById('sub-tab-' + name).classList.add('active');
  btn.classList.add('active');
}

// URLハッシュでタブを開く
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  const hash = location.hash;
  if (hash) {
    const tabName = hash.replace('#tab-', '');
    const btn = document.querySelector(`.main-tab-btn[onclick*="'${tabName}'"]`);
    if (btn) {
      document.querySelectorAll('.main-tab-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
      document.querySelectorAll('.main-tab-content').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('active'));
      document.getElementById('tab-' + tabName).classList.add('active');
      btn.classList.add('active');
    }
  }
  const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
  document.getElementById('issueDate').value = today;
  loadMaster();
  // 会話履歴はブラウザを閉じたら消える（実行ログからは確認可能）
  loadSystemStatus();
  // 実行ログ初期ロード（各タブのログをバックグラウンドで取得）
  loadExecLog('jidou');
  loadExecLog('shocho');
  loadExecLog('shiharai');
  loadChatSessionLog();
  // インラインルール動的読み込み（rules.htmlから取得）
  loadAllInlineRules();
});

// ===== インラインルール動的読み込み =====
// rules.htmlをsingle source of truthとし、index.htmlの各タブのルールセクションを動的に読み込む。
const INLINE_RULE_TABS = [
  { key: 'jidou',     rulesTabId: 'tab-jidou' },
  { key: 'assistant', rulesTabId: 'tab-assistant' },
  { key: 'shocho',    rulesTabId: 'tab-shocho' },
  { key: 'shiharai',  rulesTabId: 'tab-shiharai' },
];

async function loadAllInlineRules() {
  for (const { key, rulesTabId } of INLINE_RULE_TABS) {
    loadInlineRule(key, rulesTabId);
  }
}

async function loadInlineRule(key, rulesTabId) {
  const el = document.getElementById(`inline-rule-content-${key}`);
  if (!el) return;
  try {
    const r = await fetch(`/api/rules_html/${rulesTabId}`);
    if (!r.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${r.status}`);
    const data = await r.json();
    if (data.html) {
      // rules.htmlのタブ内容をそのまま埋め込む
      el.innerHTML = data.html;
      el.style.color = '';
      el.style.fontSize = '';
      el.style.padding = '';
    } else {
      el.innerHTML = `<div style="color:#dc3545; font-size:12px;">ルール読み込みエラー: ${data.error || '不明'}</div>`;
    }
  } catch(e) {
    if (el) el.innerHTML = `<div style="color:#dc3545; font-size:12px;">ルール取得エラー: ${e.message}</div>`;
  }
}

// ===== 自動転記 =====
async function runProcess(dbType) {
  const btnMap = { all: 'btn-all', honten: 'btn-honten', pca: 'btn-pca' };
  const btn = document.getElementById(btnMap[dbType]);
  const statusDiv = document.getElementById('process-status');
  const logDiv = document.getElementById('process-log');
  const logList = document.getElementById('log-list');

  btn.disabled = true;
  statusDiv.textContent = '⏳ 処理中...';
  document.getElementById('system-state').textContent = '処理中';
  document.getElementById('system-state').style.color = '#fd7e14';

  try {
    const r = await fetch('/run', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ db_type: dbType })
    });
    const data = await r.json();
    const color = (data.errors || 0) > 0 ? '#dc3545' : '#28a745';
    statusDiv.style.color = color;
    statusDiv.textContent = `✅ 完了: 成功${data.success || 0}件 / 要確認${data.reviews || 0}件 / エラー${data.errors || 0}件`;
    document.getElementById('process-count').textContent = (data.success || 0) + (data.reviews || 0);
    document.getElementById('system-state').textContent = '待機中';
    document.getElementById('system-state').style.color = '#17a2b8';
    loadStatusLog();
    loadExecLog('jidou', true);
  } catch(e) {
    statusDiv.style.color = '#dc3545';
    statusDiv.textContent = '❌ エラー: ' + e.message;
    loadExecLog('jidou', true);
  } finally {
    btn.disabled = false;
  }
}

// ===== システム状態 =====
async function loadSystemStatus() {
  try {
    const r = await fetch('/api/status');
    const data = await r.json();
    if (data.freee_connected) {
      document.getElementById('freee-status').textContent = '● 接続済み';
      document.getElementById('freee-status').style.color = '#28a745';
    } else {
      document.getElementById('freee-status').textContent = '● 未接続';
      document.getElementById('freee-status').style.color = '#dc3545';
    }
    if (data.process_count !== undefined) {
      document.getElementById('process-count').textContent = data.process_count;
    }
  } catch(e) {}
}

async function loadStatusLog() {
  try {
    const r = await fetch('/api/logs');
    const data = await r.json();
    const logs = data.logs || [];
    const section = document.getElementById('status-log-section');
    const list = document.getElementById('status-log-list');
    if (logs.length === 0) {
      section.style.display = 'none';
      return;
    }
    section.style.display = 'block';
    list.innerHTML = logs.map(log => {
      const color = log.status === 'success' ? '#28a745' : log.status === 'review' ? '#856404' : '#dc3545';
      const icon = log.status === 'success' ? '✅' : log.status === 'review' ? '⚠️' : '❌';
      return `<div style="padding:4px 0; border-bottom:1px solid #eee; font-size:12px;">
        <span style="color:${color};">${icon}</span>
        <span style="color:#888; margin:0 8px;">${log.time || ''}</span>
        <span>${log.message || ''}</span>
      </div>`;
    }).join('');
  } catch(e) {}
}

// ===== 仕訳プレビュー =====
let currentPreviewDb = 'all';
async function loadPreview(dbType) {
  currentPreviewDb = dbType;
  ['all','honten','pca'].forEach(t => {
    const btn = document.getElementById('prev-btn-' + t);
    btn.className = t === dbType ? 'btn btn-primary' : 'btn btn-secondary';
  });
  const loading = document.getElementById('preview-loading');
  const content = document.getElementById('preview-content');
  loading.style.display = 'block';
  content.innerHTML = '';
  try {
    const r = await fetch('/api/preview?db=' + dbType);
    const data = await r.json();
    loading.style.display = 'none';
    if (!data.previews || data.previews.length === 0) {
      content.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#888; font-size:13px; padding:16px;">対象レコードはありません。</div>';
      return;
    }
    content.innerHTML = data.previews.map(item => buildPreviewCard(item)).join('');
  } catch(e) {
    loading.style.display = 'none';
    content.innerHTML = `<div style="color:#dc3545; font-size:13px;">❌ エラー: ${e.message}</div>`;
  }
}

function buildPreviewCard(item) {
  const j = item.journal || item;
  const action = j.action || item.action;
  const borderColor = action === 'register' || action === 'register_scout_only' ? '#28a745'
    : action === 'delete' ? '#dc3545'
    : action === 'refund' ? '#fd7e14'
    : action === 'review' ? '#ffc107' : '#6c757d';
  const actionLabel = action === 'register' ? '通常登録'
    : action === 'register_scout_only' ? 'スカウト手数料のみ'
    : action === 'delete' ? '取引削除（入社前辞退）'
    : action === 'refund' ? '返金マイナス仕訳'
    : action === 'review' ? '要手動確認' : action;
  const badgeClass = action === 'register' || action === 'register_scout_only' ? 'badge-ok'
    : action === 'delete' ? 'badge-error'
    : action === 'review' || action === 'refund' ? 'badge-review' : 'badge-skip';

  let html = `<div class="card" style="margin-bottom:16px; border-left:4px solid ${borderColor};">`;
  html += `<div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:flex-start; flex-wrap:wrap; gap:8px; margin-bottom:12px;">`;
  html += `<div>
    <span style="font-size:16px; font-weight:bold;">${item.phase || ''}</span>
    <span class="badge badge-skip" style="margin-left:8px;">${item.db_type || 'honten'}</span>
    <span class="badge ${badgeClass}" style="margin-left:4px;">${actionLabel}</span>
    ${j.needs_invoice ? '<span class="badge" style="background:#17a2b8;color:#fff;margin-left:4px;">請求書登録あり</span>' : ''}
  </div>`;
  html += `<div style="font-size:12px;color:#888;">ステータス: ${j.original_status || item.original_status || '—'} / 入社日: ${item.nyusha_date || j.nyusha_date || '—'}</div>`;
  html += `</div>`;
  html += `<p style="font-size:13px;color:#555;margin-bottom:12px;">${j.message || item.message || ''}</p>`;

  if (action === 'review') {
    html += `<div class="alert alert-warning" style="font-size:13px;">⚠️ 手動で確認・処理が必要です。</div>`;
  } else if (action === 'delete') {
    html += `<div class="alert" style="background:#f8d7da;color:#721c24;border:1px solid #f5c6cb;font-size:13px;">🗑 入社前辞退のため、freeeの取引を削除します。</div>`;
  } else {
    if (j.sales_entry) html += buildEntryTable(j.sales_entry, action === 'refund' ? '▼ 売上マイナス仕訳（返金）' : '▼ 売上仕訳（収入）', action === 'refund' ? '#fd7e14' : '#28a745');
    if (j.purchase_entry) html += buildEntryTable(j.purchase_entry, action === 'refund' ? '▼ 仕入マイナス仕訳（返金）' : '▼ 仕入仕訳（支出）', action === 'refund' ? '#fd7e14' : '#dc3545');
    if (j.pca_entry) html += buildEntryTable(j.pca_entry, '▼ PCA支払仕訳（PCA仕入高）', '#6f42c1');
  }

  if (action !== 'review') {
    html += `<div style="margin-top:8px;">
      <button class="btn btn-success" style="font-size:13px;" onclick="runSinglePreview('${item.page_id}', '${item.db_type || 'honten'}', this)">▶ この1件を登録</button>
      <span id="prev-result-${item.page_id}" style="margin-left:12px;font-size:13px;"></span>
    </div>`;
  }
  html += `</div>`;
  return html;
}

function buildEntryTable(entry, label, color) {
  if (!entry || !entry.details || entry.details.length === 0) return '';
  const d = entry.details[0];
  return `<div style="margin-bottom:12px;">
    <div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:bold;color:${color};margin-bottom:4px;">${label}
      <span style="font-weight:normal;color:#555;margin-left:8px;">部門: <strong>${entry.section_name || '—'}</strong></span>
    </div>
    <table style="font-size:12px;width:100%;">
      <thead><tr><th>発生日</th><th>取引先</th><th>決済期日</th><th>勘定科目</th><th>金額</th><th>備考</th><th>メモタグ</th></tr></thead>
      <tbody><tr>
        <td>${entry.issue_date || '—'}</td>
        <td>${entry.partner_name || '—'}</td>
        <td>${entry.due_date || '—'}</td>
        <td>${d.account_item_name || '—'}</td>
        <td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold;">${(d.amount || 0).toLocaleString()}円</td>
        <td>${d.description || '—'}</td>
        <td style="color:#6f42c1;">${(d.tag_names || []).join(', ') || '—'}</td>
      </tr></tbody>
    </table>
  </div>`;
}

async function runSinglePreview(pageId, dbType, btn) {
  btn.disabled = true;
  btn.textContent = '処理中...';
  const span = document.getElementById('prev-result-' + pageId);
  try {
    const r = await fetch('/run/single', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ page_id: pageId, db_type: dbType })
    });
    const data = await r.json();
    if (data.status === 'success') {
      span.style.color = '#28a745';
      span.textContent = '✅ ' + data.message;
      btn.textContent = '✅ 登録済み';
    } else if (data.status === 'review') {
      span.style.color = '#856404';
      span.textContent = '⚠️ ' + data.message;
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = '▶ この1件を登録';
    } else {
      span.style.color = '#dc3545';
      span.textContent = '❌ ' + data.message;
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = '▶ この1件を登録';
    }
  } catch(e) {
    span.style.color = '#dc3545';
    span.textContent = 'エラー: ' + e.message;
    btn.disabled = false;
    btn.textContent = '▶ この1件を登録';
  }
}

// ===== 書類照合 =====
let _matchPreviewData = null;
async function loadMatchPreview() {
  const btn = document.getElementById('btnMatchPreview');
  const resultDiv = document.getElementById('match-result');
  btn.disabled = true;
  btn.textContent = '⏳ 照合中...';
  resultDiv.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#888;font-size:13px;">照合中...</div>';
  try {
    const r = await fetch('/api/match/preview');
    const data = await r.json();
    btn.disabled = false;
    btn.textContent = '🔍 照合プレビュー';
    if (data.error) {
      resultDiv.innerHTML = `<div style="color:#dc3545;font-size:13px;">❌ ${data.error}</div>`;
      return;
    }
    _matchPreviewData = data;
    resultDiv.innerHTML = _buildMatchHTML(data);
    document.getElementById('btnMatchExecute').style.display = '';
    document.getElementById('btnMatchReset').style.display = '';
    btn.style.display = 'none';
  } catch(e) {
    btn.disabled = false;
    btn.textContent = '🔍 照合プレビュー';
    resultDiv.innerHTML = `<div style="color:#dc3545;font-size:13px;">❌ エラー: ${e.message}</div>`;
  }
}

function _buildMatchHTML(data) {
  const matched = data.matched || [];
  const unmatched = data.unmatched || [];
  const total = data.total_receipts || 0;
  if (total === 0 && matched.length === 0 && unmatched.length === 0) {
    return '<div style="color:#888;font-size:13px;padding:12px;">未照合の書類はありません。</div>';
  }
  let html = `<div style="font-size:13px;color:#555;margin-bottom:12px;">合計${total}件の未紐づけ書類を検出。照合候補: ${matched.length}件 / 未照合: ${unmatched.length}件</div>`;
  if (matched.length > 0) {
    html += `<div style="font-weight:bold;font-size:12px;color:#28a745;margin-bottom:8px;">✅ 照合候補 (${matched.length}件)</div>`;
    matched.forEach(item => {
      const scoreColor = item.score >= 80 ? '#28a745' : item.score >= 50 ? '#ffc107' : '#dc3545';
      const receiptName = item.receipt_description || item.receipt_name || '書類';
      const breakdownHtml = (item.score_breakdown || []).map(b => `<span style="background:#d1fae5;color:#065f46;border-radius:4px;padding:1px 6px;margin-right:4px;font-size:11px;">✓ ${b}</span>`).join('');
      const warningsHtml = (item.score_warnings || []).map(w => `<span style="background:#fef3c7;color:#92400e;border-radius:4px;padding:1px 6px;margin-right:4px;font-size:11px;">⚠ ${w}</span>`).join('');
      html += `<div style="border:1px solid #dee2e6;border-radius:8px;padding:12px;margin-bottom:8px;background:#fff;">
        <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:flex-start;margin-bottom:6px;">
          <div style="font-weight:bold;font-size:13px;">📄 ${receiptName}</div>
          <span style="background:${scoreColor};color:#fff;border-radius:12px;padding:2px 10px;font-size:12px;">スコア: ${item.score}</span>
        </div>
        <div style="font-size:12px;color:#555;">
          照合先: <strong>${item.deal_partner || '—'}</strong> / ${item.deal_date || '—'} / ${(item.deal_amount || 0).toLocaleString()}円
          ${(item.deal_url || (item.deal_id ? `https://secure.freee.co.jp/deals#deal_id=${item.deal_id}` : '')) ? `<a href="${item.deal_url || `https://secure.freee.co.jp/deals#deal_id=${item.deal_id}`}" target="_blank" rel="noopener" style="margin-left:8px;font-size:11px;color:#2563eb;text-decoration:underline;">freeeで確認 ↗</a>` : ''}
        </div>
        <div style="margin-top:6px;line-height:1.8;">${breakdownHtml}</div>
        ${warningsHtml ? `<div style="margin-top:4px;line-height:1.8;">${warningsHtml}</div>` : ''}
        <div style="font-size:11px;color:#94a3b8;margin-top:4px;">書類ID: ${item.receipt_id} / 仕訳ID: ${item.deal_id}</div>
      </div>`;
    });
  }
  if (unmatched.length > 0) {
    html += `<div style="font-weight:bold;font-size:12px;color:#b45309;margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:8px;">⚠️ 未照合 (${unmatched.length}件)</div>`;
    unmatched.forEach(item => {
      const receiptName = item.description || item.receipt_name || '書類';
      const bestDealUrl = item.best_deal_url || (item.best_deal_id ? `https://secure.freee.co.jp/deals#deal_id=${item.best_deal_id}` : '');
      const bestDealLink = bestDealUrl
        ? `<a href="${bestDealUrl}" target="_blank" rel="noopener" style="color:#2563eb;text-decoration:underline;">freeeで確認 ↗</a>`
        : '';
      html += `<div style="border:1px solid #fde68a;border-radius:8px;padding:10px;margin-bottom:6px;background:#fffbeb;">
        <div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:bold;">📄 ${receiptName}</div>
        <div style="font-size:11px;color:#92400e;margin-top:4px;">理由: ${item.reason || '不明'}${item.best_score !== undefined ? ` / 最高候補スコア: ${item.best_score}点` : ''}</div>
        <div style="font-size:11px;color:#94a3b8;">書類ID: ${item.receipt_id}${item.amount ? ` / 金額: ${item.amount.toLocaleString()}円` : ''}${item.issue_date ? ` / 発行日: ${item.issue_date}` : ''}${item.best_deal_id ? ` / 候補仕訳ID: ${item.best_deal_id}` : ''} ${bestDealLink}</div>
      </div>`;
    });
  }
  return html;
}

async function executeMatch() {
  if (!_matchPreviewData) return;
  const btn = document.getElementById('btnMatchExecute');
  btn.disabled = true;
  btn.textContent = '⏳ 実行中...';
  try {
    const r = await fetch('/api/match/execute', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify(_matchPreviewData)
    });
    const data = await r.json();
    document.getElementById('match-result').innerHTML = `<div style="color:#28a745;font-size:13px;padding:12px;">✅ 完了: ${data.matched || 0}件紐づけました。</div>`;
    resetMatch();
    loadExecLog('shocho', true);
  } catch(e) {
    btn.disabled = false;
    btn.textContent = '✅ 紐づけを実行';
    loadExecLog('shocho', true);
  }
}

function resetMatch() {
  _matchPreviewData = null;
  document.getElementById('btnMatchPreview').style.display = '';
  document.getElementById('btnMatchExecute').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('btnMatchReset').style.display = 'none';
}

// ===== 支払管理 =====
let _paymentPreviewData = null;
async function loadPaymentPreview() {
  const btn = document.getElementById('btnPayPreview');
  const resultDiv = document.getElementById('payment-result');
  btn.disabled = true;
  btn.textContent = '⏳ 取得中...';
  resultDiv.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#888;font-size:13px;">取得中...</div>';
  try {
    const r = await fetch('/api/payment/preview');
    const data = await r.json();
    btn.disabled = false;
    btn.textContent = '💳 支払プレビュー';
    if (data.error) {
      resultDiv.innerHTML = `<div style="color:#dc3545;font-size:13px;">❌ ${data.error}</div>`;
      return;
    }
    _paymentPreviewData = data;
    resultDiv.innerHTML = _buildPaymentHTML(data);
    document.getElementById('btnPayReset').style.display = '';
    btn.style.display = 'none';
  } catch(e) {
    btn.disabled = false;
    btn.textContent = '💳 支払プレビュー';
    resultDiv.innerHTML = `<div style="color:#dc3545;font-size:13px;">❌ エラー: ${e.message}</div>`;
  }
}

function _buildPaymentHTML(data) {
  const groups = data.groups || [];
  const alerts = data.alerts || [];

  // アラートブロック（常に一番上）
  let alertHtml = '';
  if (alerts.length > 0) {
    alertHtml += `<div style="margin-bottom:16px;"><h4 style="font-size:13px;font-weight:bold;color:#856404;margin-bottom:8px;">⚠️ 要確認（${alerts.length}件）</h4>`;
    alerts.forEach(a => {
      const dealUrl = a.deal_id
        ? `https://secure.freee.co.jp/deals#deal_id=${a.deal_id}`
        : null;
      const linkHtml = dealUrl
        ? ` <a href="${dealUrl}" target="_blank" style="font-size:11px;color:#0d6efd;text-decoration:none;margin-left:6px;">🔗 freeeで確認</a>`
        : '';
      alertHtml += `<div style="background:#fff3cd;border:1px solid #ffc107;border-radius:6px;padding:8px 12px;margin-bottom:6px;font-size:12px;">
        ${a.partner_name || '—'} / ${a.due_date || '—'} / ${(a.amount || 0).toLocaleString()}円 — ${a.reason || ''}${linkHtml}
      </div>`;
    });
    alertHtml += '</div>';
  }

  if (groups.length === 0) {
    const noDeals = '<div style="color:#888;font-size:13px;padding:12px;">支払対象の仕訳はありません。</div>';
    return alertHtml + (alerts.length === 0 ? noDeals : '');
  }

  let html = alertHtml;
  groups.forEach(group => {
    const total = (group.deals || []).reduce((s, d) => s + (d.amount || 0), 0);
    html += `<div style="border:1px solid #dee2e6;border-radius:8px;padding:14px;margin-bottom:16px;background:#fff;">
      <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;margin-bottom:10px;">
        <div style="font-weight:bold;font-size:14px;">📅 支払期日: ${group.due_date}</div>
        <div style="font-size:13px;color:#555;">合計: <strong>${total.toLocaleString()}円</strong>（${group.deals.length}件）</div>
      </div>
      <table style="width:100%;font-size:12px;border-collapse:collapse;margin-bottom:10px;">
        <thead><tr style="background:#f8f9fa;"><th style="padding:4px 8px;text-align:left;">取引先</th><th style="padding:4px 8px;text-align:right;">金額</th><th style="padding:4px 8px;text-align:left;">備考</th></tr></thead>
        <tbody>`;
    group.deals.forEach(d => {
      const countBadge = d.count > 1 ? ` <span style="background:#e9ecef;border-radius:4px;padding:1px 6px;font-size:11px;color:#555;">${d.count}件</span>` : '';
      html += `<tr style="border-top:1px solid #eee;">
        <td style="padding:4px 8px;">${d.partner_name || '—'}${countBadge}</td>
        <td style="padding:4px 8px;text-align:right;">${(d.amount || 0).toLocaleString()}円</td>
        <td style="padding:4px 8px;color:#888;">${d.description || ''}</td>
      </tr>`;
    });
    // まとめ後の deal_ids を展開して全件分の ID を収集
    const dealIds = group.deals.flatMap(d => d.deal_ids || (d.id ? [d.id] : []));
    html += `</tbody></table>
      <button class="btn btn-success" style="font-size:12px;" onclick='downloadFBForDate("${group.due_date}", ${JSON.stringify(dealIds)})'>
        ⬇ ${group.due_date} 分の振込データをダウンロード
      </button>
    </div>`;
  });

  return html;
}

async function downloadFBForDate(dueDate, dealIds) {
  const transferDate = dueDate.replace(/-/g, '');
  const filename = `sogohurikomi_${transferDate}.txt`;
  const btns = document.querySelectorAll(`[onclick*="${dueDate}"]`);
  btns.forEach(b => b.disabled = true);
  try {
    const r = await fetch('/api/payment/generate_fb', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ transfer_date: transferDate, deal_ids: dealIds })
    });
    if (!r.ok) {
      const err = await r.json();
      alert('エラー: ' + (err.error || r.statusText));
      btns.forEach(b => b.disabled = false);
      return;
    }
    const count = r.headers.get('X-Transfer-Count') || '?';
    const amount = r.headers.get('X-Transfer-Amount') || '?';
    const tagged = r.headers.get('X-Tagged-Count') || '?';
    const blob = await r.blob();
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = url; a.download = filename; a.click();
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
    document.getElementById('payment-result').insertAdjacentHTML('afterbegin',
      `<div style="background:#d4edda;border:1px solid #c3e6cb;border-radius:6px;padding:10px 14px;font-size:12px;color:#155724;margin-bottom:10px;">✅ ${dueDate}分の振込データをダウンロードしました（${count}件 / ¥${Number(amount).toLocaleString()}）。freeeの${tagged}件の仕訳に「振込依頼済」タグを付与しました。</div>`
    );
    loadExecLog('shiharai', true);
  } catch(e) {
    alert('エラー: ' + e.message);
    btns.forEach(b => b.disabled = false);
    loadExecLog('shiharai', true);
  }
}

function resetPayment() {
  _paymentPreviewData = null;
  document.getElementById('btnPayPreview').style.display = '';
  document.getElementById('btnPayReset').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('payment-result').innerHTML = '';
}

// ===== 証憑モーダル =====
function openReceiptModal(receiptIds, partnerName) {
  const modal = document.getElementById('receipt-modal');
  const title = document.getElementById('receipt-modal-title');
  const body = document.getElementById('receipt-modal-body');
  title.textContent = `証憑確認 — ${partnerName}（${receiptIds.length}件）`;
  body.innerHTML = '<div style="text-align:center;padding:20px;color:#888;">読み込み中...</div>';
  modal.style.display = 'flex';
  let html = '';
  if (receiptIds.length > 1) {
    html += '<div style="display:flex;gap:6px;margin-bottom:10px;flex-wrap:wrap;">';
    receiptIds.forEach((id, i) => {
      html += `<button onclick="switchReceiptTab(${i})" id="rtab-${i}" style="padding:4px 12px;font-size:12px;border:1px solid #28a745;border-radius:4px;background:${i===0?'#28a745':'#fff'};color:${i===0?'#fff':'#28a745'};cursor:pointer;">証憑 ${i+1}</button>`;
    });
    html += '</div>';
  }
  receiptIds.forEach((id, i) => {
    html += `<div id="rpanel-${i}" style="display:${i===0?'block':'none'};">
      <div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-bottom:8px;justify-content:flex-end;">
        <a href="/api/receipt/${id}/download?inline=1" target="_blank" style="font-size:12px;padding:4px 10px;background:#17a2b8;color:#fff;border-radius:4px;text-decoration:none;">🔍 別タブで開く</a>
        <a href="/api/receipt/${id}/download" download style="font-size:12px;padding:4px 10px;background:#6c757d;color:#fff;border-radius:4px;text-decoration:none;">⬇ ダウンロード</a>
      </div>
      <iframe src="/api/receipt/${id}/download?inline=1" style="width:100%;height:520px;border:1px solid #dee2e6;border-radius:4px;"></iframe>
    </div>`;
  });
  body.innerHTML = html;
}

function switchReceiptTab(idx) {
  document.querySelectorAll('[id^="rpanel-"]').forEach((p, i) => p.style.display = i === idx ? 'block' : 'none');
  document.querySelectorAll('[id^="rtab-"]').forEach((t, i) => {
    t.style.background = i === idx ? '#28a745' : '#fff';
    t.style.color = i === idx ? '#fff' : '#28a745';
  });
}

function closeReceiptModal() {
  document.getElementById('receipt-modal').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('receipt-modal-body').innerHTML = '';
}

document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
  if (e.target === document.getElementById('receipt-modal')) closeReceiptModal();
});

// ===== 仕訳アシスタント（マスタ・フォーム・AI） =====
let masterData = { sections: [], tags: [], account_items: [], partners: [] };

// 部門名を「親部門：子部門」形式で表示するヘルパー
function displaySectionName(sectionName) {
  if (!sectionName || !masterData.sections.length) return sectionName || '-';
  const sec = masterData.sections.find(s => s.name === sectionName);
  if (sec && sec.parent_id) {
    const parent = masterData.sections.find(p => p.id === sec.parent_id);
    if (parent) return `${parent.name}：${sec.name}`;
  }
  return sectionName;
}
let aiHistory = [];
let aiFiles = [];
let formFiles = [];

function getOrCreateSessionId() {
  let sid = sessionStorage.getItem('ai_session_id');
  if (!sid) {
    sid = 'sess_' + Date.now() + '_' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8);
    sessionStorage.setItem('ai_session_id', sid);
  }
  return sid;
}

async function loadChatHistory() {
  const sid = getOrCreateSessionId();
  try {
    const res = await fetch(`/api/chat_history/${sid}`);
    const data = await res.json();
    if (data.messages && data.messages.length > 0) {
      aiHistory = data.messages;
      const container = document.getElementById('aiMessages');
      container.innerHTML = '';
      data.messages.forEach(msg => {
        if (msg.role !== 'system') addAiMessage(msg.role === 'user' ? 'user' : 'assistant', msg.content);
      });
    }
  } catch(e) {}
}

async function saveChatHistory() {
  const sid = getOrCreateSessionId();
  try {
    await fetch(`/api/chat_history/${sid}`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ messages: aiHistory }),
    });
  } catch(e) {}
}

async function deleteChatHistory() {
  const sid = getOrCreateSessionId();
  try { await fetch(`/api/chat_history/${sid}`, { method: 'DELETE' }); } catch(e) {}
}

async function loadMaster() {
  try {
    const res = await fetch('/api/freee_master');
    const data = await res.json();
    if (data.error) return;
    masterData = data;
    const dl = document.getElementById('partnerList');
    dl.innerHTML = '';
    data.partners.forEach(p => {
      const opt = document.createElement('option');
      opt.value = p.name;
      dl.appendChild(opt);
    });
    addDetailRow();
  } catch(e) { addDetailRow(); }
}

function toggleRepeat() {
  const enabled = document.getElementById('repeatEnabled').checked;
  document.getElementById('repeatOptions').style.display = enabled ? 'block' : 'none';
  if (enabled) updateRepeatPreview();
  else document.getElementById('repeatPreview').style.display = 'none';
}

function updateRepeatPreview() {
  if (!document.getElementById('repeatEnabled').checked) return;
  const issueDate = document.getElementById('issueDate').value;
  const dueDate = document.getElementById('dueDate').value;
  const count = parseInt(document.getElementById('repeatCount').value) || 1;
  if (!issueDate) return;
  const previewEl = document.getElementById('repeatPreview');
  const listEl = document.getElementById('repeatPreviewList');
  previewEl.style.display = 'block';
  const rows = [];
  const base = new Date(issueDate);
  const baseDue = dueDate ? new Date(dueDate) : null;
  for (let i = 0; i < Math.min(count, 24); i++) {
    const d = new Date(base.getFullYear(), base.getMonth() + i, base.getDate());
    const lastDay = new Date(d.getFullYear(), d.getMonth() + 1, 0).getDate();
    if (d.getDate() > lastDay) d.setDate(lastDay);
    let dueStr = '-';
    if (baseDue) {
      const due = new Date(baseDue.getFullYear(), baseDue.getMonth() + i, baseDue.getDate());
      const dueLastDay = new Date(due.getFullYear(), due.getMonth() + 1, 0).getDate();
      if (due.getDate() > dueLastDay) due.setDate(dueLastDay);
      dueStr = due.toISOString().split('T')[0];
    }
    rows.push(`<span style="display:inline-block;margin-right:16px;margin-bottom:4px;">${i+1}回目: <strong>${d.toISOString().split('T')[0]}</strong>${dueStr !== '-' ? ` → 決済: <strong>${dueStr}</strong>` : ''}</span>`);
  }
  if (count > 24) rows.push(`<span style="color:#888;font-size:11px;">… 他 ${count - 24} 件</span>`);
  listEl.innerHTML = rows.join('');
}

function addDetailRow() {
  const container = document.getElementById('detailRows');
  let accountOptions = '<option value="">勘定科目を選択</option>';
  masterData.account_items.forEach(a => { accountOptions += `<option value="${a.name}">${a.name}</option>`; });
  let sectionOptions = '<option value="">部門なし</option>';
  masterData.sections.forEach(s => { sectionOptions += `<option value="${s.name}">${s.name}</option>`; });
  let tagOptions = masterData.tags.map(t => `<option value="${t.name}">${t.name}</option>`).join('');
  const row = document.createElement('div');
  row.className = 'detail-row';
  row.innerHTML = `
    <button type="button" class="remove-btn" onclick="removeDetailRow(this)">✕</button>
    <div class="form-row">
      <div class="form-group flex-2"><label>勘定科目 *</label><select name="account_item_name" required>${accountOptions}</select></div>
      <div class="form-group flex-1"><label>税抜金額 *</label><input type="number" name="amount" placeholder="例: 100000" required min="0"></div>
      <div class="form-group flex-1"><label>税区分コード</label>
        <select name="tax_code">
          <option value="1">課税売上10%（1）</option>
          <option value="7">課税仕入10%（7）</option>
          <option value="0">不課税（0）</option>
          <option value="3">非課税売上（3）</option>
        </select>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="form-row">
      <div class="form-group flex-2"><label>部門</label><select name="section_name">${sectionOptions}</select></div>
      <div class="form-group flex-2"><label>メモタグ</label><select name="tag_name"><option value="">タグなし</option>${tagOptions}</select></div>
      <div class="form-group flex-3"><label>備考</label><input type="text" name="description" placeholder="備考（任意）"></div>
    </div>`;
  container.appendChild(row);
}

function removeDetailRow(btn) {
  const row = btn.closest('.detail-row');
  if (document.getElementById('detailRows').children.length > 1) row.remove();
}

function handleFormFileSelect(input) {
  for (const file of input.files) {
    if (!formFiles.find(f => f.name === file.name && f.size === file.size)) formFiles.push(file);
  }
  renderFormFileList(); input.value = '';
}

function renderFormFileList() {
  const listEl = document.getElementById('formFileList');
  if (formFiles.length === 0) { listEl.innerHTML = ''; return; }
  listEl.innerHTML = formFiles.map((f, i) => `<div class="file-item"><span>📄</span><span class="file-name">${f.name}</span><span style="font-size:11px;color:#666;">${(f.size/1024).toFixed(0)} KB</span><button class="file-remove" onclick="removeFormFile(${i})">✕</button></div>`).join('');
}

function removeFormFile(idx) { formFiles.splice(idx, 1); renderFormFileList(); }

function handleDragOver(e, zoneId) { e.preventDefault(); document.getElementById(zoneId).classList.add('dragover'); }
function handleDragLeave(zoneId) { document.getElementById(zoneId).classList.remove('dragover'); }
function handleDrop(e, inputId) {
  e.preventDefault();
  document.getElementById('formDropZone').classList.remove('dragover');
  for (const file of e.dataTransfer.files) {
    if (!formFiles.find(f => f.name === file.name && f.size === file.size)) formFiles.push(file);
  }
  renderFormFileList();
}

function handleAiDragOver(e) { e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation(); document.getElementById('aiFileZone').classList.add('dragover'); }
function handleAiDragLeave(e) {
  e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation();
  if (!document.getElementById('aiFileZone').contains(e.relatedTarget)) document.getElementById('aiFileZone').classList.remove('dragover');
}
function handleAiDrop(e) {
  e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation();
  document.getElementById('aiFileZone').classList.remove('dragover');
  for (const file of e.dataTransfer.files) {
    if (!aiFiles.find(f => f.name === file.name && f.size === file.size)) aiFiles.push(file);
  }
  renderAiFileList();
}
function handleAiFileSelect(input) {
  for (const file of input.files) {
    if (!aiFiles.find(f => f.name === file.name && f.size === file.size)) aiFiles.push(file);
  }
  renderAiFileList(); input.value = '';
}
function renderAiFileList() {
  const listEl = document.getElementById('aiFileList');
  const badge = document.getElementById('aiFileBadge');
  if (aiFiles.length === 0) { listEl.style.display = 'none'; badge.style.display = 'none'; return; }
  badge.textContent = `${aiFiles.length}件`; badge.style.display = 'inline-block';
  listEl.style.display = 'block';
  listEl.innerHTML = aiFiles.map((f, i) => `<div class="file-item"><span>📄</span><span class="file-name">${f.name}</span><span style="font-size:11px;color:#666;">${(f.size/1024).toFixed(0)} KB</span><button class="file-remove" onclick="removeAiFile(${i})">✕</button></div>`).join('');
}
function removeAiFile(idx) { aiFiles.splice(idx, 1); renderAiFileList(); }

async function submitForm() {
  const btn = document.getElementById('formSubmitBtn');
  const spinner = document.getElementById('formSpinner');
  const resultBox = document.getElementById('formResult');
  const issueDate = document.getElementById('issueDate').value;
  const dueDate = document.getElementById('dueDate').value;
  const dealType = document.getElementById('dealType').value;
  const partnerName = document.getElementById('partnerName').value;
  const repeatEnabled = document.getElementById('repeatEnabled').checked;
  const repeatCount = parseInt(document.getElementById('repeatCount').value) || 1;
  if (!issueDate) { alert('発生日を入力してください'); return; }
  const detailRows = document.querySelectorAll('#detailRows .detail-row');
  const details = [];
  for (const row of detailRows) {
    const accountName = row.querySelector('[name="account_item_name"]').value;
    const amount = parseInt(row.querySelector('[name="amount"]').value);
    const taxCode = parseInt(row.querySelector('[name="tax_code"]').value);
    const sectionName = row.querySelector('[name="section_name"]').value;
    const tagName = row.querySelector('[name="tag_name"]').value;
    const description = row.querySelector('[name="description"]').value;
    if (!accountName || !amount) { alert('勘定科目と金額は必須です'); return; }
    const detail = { account_item_name: accountName, amount, tax_code: taxCode, description, tag_names: tagName ? [tagName] : [] };
    if (sectionName) detail.section_name = sectionName;
    details.push(detail);
  }
  btn.disabled = true; spinner.classList.add('active'); resultBox.style.display = 'none';
  try {
    const res = await fetch('/api/assistant/register', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ deal_type: dealType, issue_date: issueDate, due_date: dueDate || null, partner_name: partnerName || null, details, repeat: repeatEnabled, repeat_count: repeatCount })
    });
    const data = await res.json();
    if (data.status === 'ok') {
      let receiptMsg = '';
      if (formFiles.length > 0 && data.ids && data.ids.length > 0) {
        const uploadResult = await uploadReceiptsToDeals(formFiles, data.ids);
        receiptMsg = `<br>📎 証憑: ${uploadResult}`;
      }
      resultBox.className = 'result-box success';
      resultBox.innerHTML = `✅ 登録完了！${data.registered}件登録しました。<br>${data.ids ? `登録ID: ${data.ids.join(', ')}` : ''}${receiptMsg}`;
      formFiles = []; renderFormFileList();
    } else {
      resultBox.className = 'result-box error';
      resultBox.innerHTML = `❌ エラー: ${data.message || JSON.stringify(data)}`;
    }
    resultBox.style.display = 'block';
  } catch(e) {
    resultBox.className = 'result-box error';
    resultBox.innerHTML = `❌ 通信エラー: ${e.message}`;
    resultBox.style.display = 'block';
  } finally {
    btn.disabled = false; spinner.classList.remove('active');
  }
}

async function uploadReceiptsToDeals(files, dealIds) {
  // ファイルが1件・仕訳が複数の場合: 全仕訳に同じファイルを紐付ける
  // ファイルが複数・仕訳が複数の場合: ファイル数 >= 仕訳数ならi番目のファイルをi番目の仕訳に、
  //   ファイル数 < 仕訳数なら全仕訳に全ファイルをアップロード
  const results = [];
  const targets = [];
  if (files.length === 1) {
    // 1ファイル → 全仕訳に紐付け
    for (const dealId of dealIds) targets.push({ file: files[0], dealId });
  } else if (files.length >= dealIds.length) {
    // ファイル数 >= 仕訳数 → i番目のファイルをi番目の仕訳に
    for (let i = 0; i < dealIds.length; i++) targets.push({ file: files[i], dealId: dealIds[i] });
    // 余ったファイルは最後の仕訳に紐付け
    for (let i = dealIds.length; i < files.length; i++) targets.push({ file: files[i], dealId: dealIds[dealIds.length - 1] });
  } else {
    // ファイル数 < 仕訳数 → 全ファイルを全仕訳に紐付け
    for (const dealId of dealIds) {
      for (const file of files) targets.push({ file, dealId });
    }
  }
  for (const { file, dealId } of targets) {
    try {
      const formData = new FormData();
      formData.append('file', file);
      formData.append('deal_id', dealId);
      formData.append('description', file.name);
      const res = await fetch('/api/assistant/upload_receipt', { method: 'POST', body: formData });
      const data = await res.json();
      results.push(data.status === 'ok' ? `${file.name}→ID:${dealId} ✅` : `${file.name}→ID:${dealId} ❌(${data.message})`);
    } catch(e) { results.push(`${file.name}→ID:${dealId} ❌(通信エラー)`); }
  }
  return results.join(', ');
}

function handleAiKey(e) { if (e.key === 'Enter' && (e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey)) sendAiMessage(); }

function addAiMessage(role, text) {
  const container = document.getElementById('aiMessages');
  const div = document.createElement('div');
  div.className = `ai-msg ${role}`;
  div.innerHTML = text.replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
  container.appendChild(div);
  container.scrollTop = container.scrollHeight;
  return div;
}

function clearAiChat() {
  aiHistory = []; aiFiles = []; renderAiFileList(); deleteChatHistory();
  document.getElementById('aiMessages').innerHTML = `<div class="ai-msg assistant">チャット履歴をクリアしました。新しい仕訳の指示をどうぞ。</div>`;
}

async function sendAiMessage() {
  const input = document.getElementById('aiInput');
  const btn = document.getElementById('aiSendBtn');
  const message = input.value.trim();
  if (!message && aiFiles.length === 0) return;
  const displayMsg = message + (aiFiles.length > 0 ? ` 📎 ${aiFiles.map(f=>f.name).join(', ')}` : '');
  addAiMessage('user', displayMsg);
  input.value = ''; btn.disabled = true;
  const thinkingDiv = addAiMessage('assistant', '⏳ 考え中...');
  try {
    let fileContents = [];
    if (aiFiles.length > 0) {
      thinkingDiv.innerHTML = '⏳ ファイルを読み取り中...';
      const formData = new FormData();
      for (const file of aiFiles) formData.append('files', file);
      formData.append('message', message);
      const extractRes = await fetch('/api/assistant/extract_file', { method: 'POST', body: formData });
      const extractData = await extractRes.json();
      if (extractData.contents) fileContents = extractData.contents;
      thinkingDiv.innerHTML = '⏳ AIが仕訳を提案中...';
    }
    const aiMessage = fileContents.length > 0 ? `${message}\n\n【添付ファイルの内容】\n${fileContents.join('\n\n---\n\n')}` : message;
    const res = await fetch('/api/assistant/ai', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ message: aiMessage, history: aiHistory, master: masterData })
    });
    const data = await res.json();
    thinkingDiv.remove();
    if (data.error) {
      addAiMessage('error', `❌ エラー: ${data.error}`);
    } else {
      aiHistory.push({ role: 'user', content: aiMessage });
      aiHistory.push({ role: 'assistant', content: data.reply });
      saveChatHistory();
      let replyHtml = data.reply.replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
      if (data.entries && data.entries.length > 0) {
        replyHtml += `<br><br><div class="preview-table"><table><tr><th>発生日</th><th>期日</th><th>種別</th><th>取引先</th><th>勘定科目</th><th>金額</th><th>部門</th><th>備考</th></tr>`;
        data.entries.forEach(e => {
          e.details.forEach(d => {
            const rawSec = d.section_name || e.section_name || '';
            const secDisplay = displaySectionName(rawSec);
            replyHtml += `<tr><td>${e.issue_date}</td><td>${e.due_date||'-'}</td><td>${e.deal_type==='income'?'収入':'支出'}</td><td>${e.partner_name||'-'}</td><td>${d.account_item_name}</td><td>${d.amount.toLocaleString()}円</td><td>${secDisplay}</td><td>${d.description||'-'}</td></tr>`;
          });
        });
        replyHtml += `</table></div><br>`;
        const hasFiles = aiFiles.length > 0;
        const entriesJson = JSON.stringify(data.entries).replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
        if (hasFiles) replyHtml += `<div style="font-size:12px;color:#555;margin-bottom:8px;">📎 添付ファイル（${aiFiles.length}件）も証憑として一緒にアップロードされます</div>`;
        replyHtml += `<button class="btn btn-success" onclick='registerAiEntries(${entriesJson})'>▶ この内容でfreeeに登録する（${data.entries.length}件）</button>`;
        if (hasFiles) replyHtml += ` <button class="btn btn-secondary" style="font-size:12px;" onclick='registerAiEntries(${entriesJson}, false)'>証憑なしで登録</button>`;
      }
      if (data.delete_actions && data.delete_actions.length > 0) {
        data.delete_actions.forEach(action => {
          const actionJson = JSON.stringify(action).replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
          const targetLabel = action.target === 'deal' ? '仕訳' : action.target === 'invoice' ? '請求書' : '仕訳・請求書';
          const dateRange = (action.start_date || '') + (action.end_date ? ` 〜 ${action.end_date}` : '');
          replyHtml += `<br><div style="border:1px solid #f5c6cb;background:#fff5f5;border-radius:8px;padding:12px;margin-top:8px;">
            <div style="font-weight:bold;color:#c0392b;margin-bottom:8px;">🗑 削除対象の検索</div>
            <div style="font-size:13px;margin-bottom:8px;">対象: <b>${targetLabel}</b> | 取引先: <b>${action.partner_name||'指定なし'}</b> | 期間: <b>${dateRange||'今年度'}</b></div>
            <button class="btn btn-warning" onclick='previewDeleteAction(${actionJson})'>🔍 削除対象を検索する</button>
          </div>`;
        });
      }
      if (data.pending_deletes && (data.pending_deletes.deal_ids.length > 0 || data.pending_deletes.invoice_ids.length > 0)) {
        const pd = data.pending_deletes;
        replyHtml += `<br><br><div style="border:1px solid #f5c6cb;background:#fff5f5;border-radius:8px;padding:12px;margin-top:8px;">
          <div style="font-weight:bold;color:#c0392b;margin-bottom:8px;">⚠️ 削除確認</div>
          <div style="font-size:13px;margin-bottom:8px;">${pd.message}</div>`;
        if ((pd.deals_detail||[]).length > 0) {
          replyHtml += `<div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:bold;color:#555;margin-bottom:4px;">仕訳 ${pd.deals_detail.length}件:</div>
            <table style="font-size:12px;border-collapse:collapse;width:100%;margin-bottom:8px;">
            <tr style="background:#f0f0f0;"><th style="padding:3px 8px;text-align:left;">日付</th><th style="padding:3px 8px;text-align:right;">金額</th><th style="padding:3px 8px;text-align:left;">取引先</th></tr>`;
          [...pd.deals_detail].sort((a,b)=>(a.issue_date||'').localeCompare(b.issue_date||'')).forEach(d => { replyHtml += `<tr><td style="padding:3px 8px;">${d.issue_date||'-'}</td><td style="padding:3px 8px;text-align:right;">${d.amount?d.amount.toLocaleString()+'円':'-'}</td><td style="padding:3px 8px;">${d.partner_name||'-'}</td></tr>`; });
          replyHtml += `</table>`;
        }
        if ((pd.invoices_detail||[]).length > 0) {
          replyHtml += `<div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:bold;color:#555;margin-bottom:4px;">請求書 ${pd.invoices_detail.length}件:</div>
            <table style="font-size:12px;border-collapse:collapse;width:100%;margin-bottom:8px;">
            <tr style="background:#f0f0f0;"><th style="padding:3px 8px;text-align:left;">請求日</th><th style="padding:3px 8px;text-align:right;">金額</th><th style="padding:3px 8px;text-align:left;">請求書番号</th></tr>`;
          [...pd.invoices_detail].sort((a,b)=>(a.billing_date||'').localeCompare(b.billing_date||'')).forEach(inv => { replyHtml += `<tr><td style="padding:3px 8px;">${inv.billing_date||'-'}</td><td style="padding:3px 8px;text-align:right;">${inv.total_amount?inv.total_amount.toLocaleString()+'円':'-'}</td><td style="padding:3px 8px;">${inv.invoice_number||'-'}</td></tr>`; });
          replyHtml += `</table>`;
        }
        const pdJson = JSON.stringify(pd).replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
        replyHtml += `<div style="margin-top:10px;"><button class="btn btn-danger" onclick='executePendingDeletes(${pdJson})'>🗑️ 削除を実行する</button> <span style="font-size:11px;color:#666;">→ 削除後は元に戻せません</span></div></div>`;
      }
      if (data.registered_ids && data.registered_ids.length > 0) {
        const regLinks = data.registered_ids.map(id => `<a href="https://secure.freee.co.jp/deals#deal_id=${id}" target="_blank" rel="noopener" style="color:#2563eb;">${id} ↗</a>`).join(', ');
        replyHtml += `<br><div style="color:#27ae60;font-weight:bold;">✅ ${data.registered_ids.length}件をfreeeに登録しました（ID: ${regLinks}）</div>`;
      }
      if (data.pending_registers && data.pending_registers.length > 0) {
        const pr = data.pending_registers;
        replyHtml += `<br><br><div style="border:1px solid #b8daff;background:#f0f7ff;border-radius:8px;padding:12px;margin-top:8px;">
          <div style="font-weight:bold;color:#1a5276;margin-bottom:8px;">✏️ 登録内容の確認</div>`;
        pr.forEach((item, idx) => {
          const args = item.deal_args || {};
          const typeLabel = item.deal_type === 'income' ? '収入' : '支出';
          const dueDateStr = args.due_date ? ` / 期日: ${args.due_date}` : '';
          replyHtml += `<div style="font-size:13px;margin-bottom:6px;"><b>${idx+1}.</b> ${args.issue_date||'-'} / ${typeLabel} / ${args.partner_name||'-'}${dueDateStr}`;
          if (args.details && args.details.length > 0) {
            replyHtml += `<table style="font-size:12px;border-collapse:collapse;width:100%;margin-top:4px;">
              <tr style="background:#dbeafe;"><th style="padding:3px 8px;text-align:left;">勘定科目</th><th style="padding:3px 8px;text-align:right;">金額</th><th style="padding:3px 8px;text-align:left;">部門</th><th style="padding:3px 8px;text-align:left;">備考</th></tr>`;
            args.details.forEach(d => {
              // 部門名: 親部門：子部門形式で表示
              const rawSection = d.section_name || args.section_name || '';
              const sectionDisplay = displaySectionName(rawSection);
              replyHtml += `<tr><td style="padding:3px 8px;">${d.account_item_name||'-'}</td><td style="padding:3px 8px;text-align:right;">${(d.amount||0).toLocaleString()}円</td><td style="padding:3px 8px;">${sectionDisplay}</td><td style="padding:3px 8px;">${d.description||'-'}</td></tr>`;
            });
            replyHtml += `</table>`;
          }
          replyHtml += `</div>`;
        });
        const prJson = JSON.stringify(pr).replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
        replyHtml += `<div style="margin-top:10px;"><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick='executeRegister(${prJson})'>▶ この内容でfreeeに登録する（${pr.length}件）</button> <span style="font-size:11px;color:#666;">→ 登録後は手動での修正が必要です</span></div></div>`;
      }
      addAiMessage('assistant', replyHtml);
    }
    aiFiles = []; renderAiFileList();
  } catch(e) {
    thinkingDiv.remove();
    addAiMessage('error', `❌ 通信エラー: ${e.message}`);
  } finally {
    btn.disabled = false;
  }
}

async function executeRegister(pendingRegisters) {
  const resultDiv = addAiMessage('assistant', '⏳ freeeに登録中...');
  try {
    const res = await fetch('/api/assistant/execute_register', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ pending_registers: pendingRegisters })
    });
    const data = await res.json();
    resultDiv.remove();
    if (data.status === 'ok') {
      const idLinks = (data.ids||[]).map(id => `<a href="https://secure.freee.co.jp/deals#deal_id=${id}" target="_blank" rel="noopener" style="color:#2563eb;">${id} ↗</a>`).join(', ');
      let msg = `✅ 登録完了！${data.registered}件をfreeeに登録しました。<br>登録ID: ${idLinks}`;
      if (data.failed && data.failed.length > 0) msg += `<br>⚠️ 失敗: ${data.failed.length}件`;
      addAiMessage('assistant', msg);
    } else {
      addAiMessage('error', `❌ 登録エラー: ${data.message || JSON.stringify(data)}`);
    }
  } catch(e) {
    resultDiv.remove();
    addAiMessage('error', `❌ 通信エラー: ${e.message}`);
  }
}

async function previewDeleteAction(action) {
  const loadingDiv = addAiMessage('assistant', '⏳ 削除対象を検索中...');
  try {
    const res = await fetch('/api/assistant/search_delete', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ action })
    });
    const data = await res.json();
    loadingDiv.remove();
    if (data.error) { addAiMessage('error', `❌ 検索エラー: ${data.error}`); return; }
    const deals = data.deals || [];
    const invoices = data.invoices || [];
    const total = deals.length + invoices.length;
    if (total === 0) { addAiMessage('assistant', 'ℹ️ 削除対象の仕訳・請求書が見つかりませんでした。'); return; }
    let html = `<div style="border:1px solid #f5c6cb;background:#fff5f5;border-radius:8px;padding:12px;">
      <div style="font-weight:bold;color:#c0392b;margin-bottom:8px;">⚠️ 削除対象：${total}件</div>
      <div style="max-height:300px;overflow-y:auto;">`;
    if (deals.length > 0) {
      html += `<div style="font-weight:bold;margin:8px 0 4px;">取引（仕訳） ${deals.length}件</div>
        <table style="width:100%;font-size:12px;border-collapse:collapse;">
        <tr style="background:#f8d7da;"><th style="padding:4px;text-align:left;"><input type="checkbox" id="chk_all_deals" onchange="toggleAll('deal')"> 全選</th><th>発生日</th><th>取引先</th><th>金額</th><th>種別</th></tr>`;
      deals.forEach(d => { html += `<tr><td><input type="checkbox" class="chk_deal" value="${d.id}" checked></td><td>${d.issue_date||'-'}</td><td>${d.partner_name||'-'}</td><td>${(d.amount||0).toLocaleString()}円</td><td>${d.type==='income'?'収入':'支出'}</td></tr>`; });
      html += `</table>`;
    }
    if (invoices.length > 0) {
      html += `<div style="font-weight:bold;margin:8px 0 4px;">請求書 ${invoices.length}件</div>
        <table style="width:100%;font-size:12px;border-collapse:collapse;">
        <tr style="background:#f8d7da;"><th style="padding:4px;text-align:left;"><input type="checkbox" id="chk_all_invoices" onchange="toggleAll('invoice')"> 全選</th><th>発生日</th><th>取引先</th><th>金額</th><th>請求書番号</th></tr>`;
      invoices.forEach(inv => { html += `<tr><td><input type="checkbox" class="chk_invoice" value="${inv.id}" checked></td><td>${inv.issue_date||'-'}</td><td>${inv.partner_name||'-'}</td><td>${(inv.total_amount||0).toLocaleString()}円</td><td>${inv.invoice_number||'-'}</td></tr>`; });
      html += `</table>`;
    }
    html += `</div><div style="margin-top:12px;"><button class="btn btn-danger" onclick="executeDeleteSelected()">🗑️ チェックした項目を削除する</button> <span style="font-size:11px;color:#666;">→ 削除後は元に戻せません</span></div></div>`;
    addAiMessage('assistant', html);
  } catch(e) { loadingDiv.remove(); addAiMessage('error', `❌ 通信エラー: ${e.message}`); }
}

function toggleAll(type) {
  const allChk = document.getElementById(`chk_all_${type}s`);
  document.querySelectorAll(`.chk_${type}`).forEach(c => c.checked = allChk.checked);
}

async function executeDeleteSelected() {
  const dealIds = [...document.querySelectorAll('.chk_deal:checked')].map(c => c.value);
  const invoiceIds = [...document.querySelectorAll('.chk_invoice:checked')].map(c => c.value);
  if (dealIds.length === 0 && invoiceIds.length === 0) { alert('削除する項目を選択してください。'); return; }
  if (!confirm(`以下を削除します。よろしいですか？\n仕訳: ${dealIds.length}件 / 請求書: ${invoiceIds.length}件`)) return;
  const loadingDiv = addAiMessage('assistant', '⏳ 削除中...');
  try {
    const res = await fetch('/api/assistant/execute_delete', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ deal_ids: dealIds, invoice_ids: invoiceIds })
    });
    const data = await res.json();
    loadingDiv.remove();
    let msg = `✅ 削除完了！`;
    if (data.deleted_deals.length > 0) msg += `<br>仕訳: ${data.deleted_deals.length}件削除`;
    if (data.deleted_invoices.length > 0) msg += `<br>請求書: ${data.deleted_invoices.length}件取消`;
    if ((data.skipped_deals||[]).length > 0) msg += `<br>ℹ️ 仕訳${data.skipped_deals.length}件は請求書連携のためスキップ`;
    if (data.failed_deals.length > 0) msg += `<br>⚠️ 仕訳削除失敗: ${data.failed_deals.map(f=>f.id).join(', ')}`;
    if (data.failed_invoices.length > 0) msg += `<br>⚠️ 請求書取消失敗: ${data.failed_invoices.map(f=>f.id).join(', ')}`;
    addAiMessage('assistant', msg);
  } catch(e) { loadingDiv.remove(); addAiMessage('error', `❌ 通信エラー: ${e.message}`); }
}

async function executePendingDeletes(pd) {
  const dealIds = pd.deal_ids || [];
  const invoiceIds = pd.invoice_ids || [];
  if (!confirm(`以下を削除します。よろしいですか？\n仕訳: ${dealIds.length}件 / 請求書: ${invoiceIds.length}件\n\n削除後は元に戻せません。`)) return;
  const loadingDiv = addAiMessage('assistant', '⏳ 削除中...');
  try {
    const res = await fetch('/api/assistant/execute_delete', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ deal_ids: dealIds.map(String), invoice_ids: invoiceIds.map(String) })
    });
    const data = await res.json();
    loadingDiv.remove();
    let msg = `✅ 削除完了！`;
    if ((data.deleted_deals||[]).length > 0) msg += `<br>仕訳: ${data.deleted_deals.length}件削除`;
    if ((data.deleted_invoices||[]).length > 0) msg += `<br>請求書: ${data.deleted_invoices.length}件取消`;
    if ((data.skipped_deals||[]).length > 0) msg += `<br>ℹ️ 仕訳${data.skipped_deals.length}件は請求書連携のためスキップ`;
    if ((data.failed_deals||[]).length > 0) msg += `<br>⚠️ 仕訳削除失敗: ${data.failed_deals.map(f=>f.id).join(', ')}`;
    if ((data.failed_invoices||[]).length > 0) msg += `<br>⚠️ 請求書取消失敗: ${data.failed_invoices.map(f=>f.id).join(', ')}`;
    addAiMessage('assistant', msg);
  } catch(e) { loadingDiv.remove(); addAiMessage('error', `❌ 通信エラー: ${e.message}`); }
}

// ===== 実行ログ（永続） =====
// tabName: 'jidou' | 'shocho' | 'shiharai'
const LOG_TYPE_MAP = { jidou: 'auto_transfer', shocho: 'invoice_match', shiharai: 'payment_fb' };
const _execLogLoaded = { jidou: false, shocho: false, shiharai: false };

async function loadExecLog(tabName, forceReload = false) {
  const logType = LOG_TYPE_MAP[tabName];
  if (!logType) return;
  const listEl = document.getElementById('exec-log-list-' + tabName);
  const countEl = document.getElementById('exec-log-count-' + tabName);
  if (!listEl) return;
  if (!forceReload && _execLogLoaded[tabName]) return;
  try {
    const r = await fetch(`/api/execution_logs?log_type=${logType}&limit=50`);
    const data = await r.json();
    const logs = data.logs || [];
    _execLogLoaded[tabName] = true;
    if (countEl) countEl.textContent = logs.length > 0 ? `（${logs.length}件）` : '';
    if (logs.length === 0) {
      listEl.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#94a3b8; font-size:12px; padding:8px 0;">実行履歴なし</div>';
      return;
    }
    listEl.innerHTML = logs.map((log, idx) => buildExecLogEntry(log, tabName, idx)).join('');
  } catch(e) {
    if (listEl) listEl.innerHTML = `<div style="color:#dc3545; font-size:12px; padding:8px 0;">ログ取得エラー: ${e.message}</div>`;
  }
}

function toggleExecLog(tabName) {
  const toggle = document.getElementById('exec-log-toggle-' + tabName);
  const body = document.getElementById('exec-log-body-' + tabName);
  if (!toggle || !body) return;
  const isOpen = body.classList.contains('open');
  if (isOpen) {
    body.classList.remove('open');
    toggle.classList.remove('open');
  } else {
    body.classList.add('open');
    toggle.classList.add('open');
    // 初回開展時にログをロード
    if (tabName === 'assistant') {
      loadChatSessionLog();
    } else {
      loadExecLog(tabName);
    }
  }
}

function toggleExecLogEntry(tabName, idx) {
  const body = document.getElementById(`exec-log-entry-body-${tabName}-${idx}`);
  if (!body) return;
  body.classList.toggle('open');
}

function buildExecLogEntry(log, tabName, idx) {
  const hasErr = log.has_error;
  const statusBadge = hasErr
    ? '<span class="exec-log-badge-err">❌ エラーあり</span>'
    : '<span class="exec-log-badge-ok">✅ 成功</span>';
  const triggerBadge = log.trigger === 'auto'
    ? '<span class="exec-log-badge-auto">自動</span>'
    : '<span class="exec-log-badge-manual">手動</span>';
  const summary = log.summary || {};
  const summaryText = buildSummaryText(tabName, summary);
  const detailHtml = buildDetailHtml(tabName, log.detail || {});
  return `
    <div class="exec-log-entry">
      <div class="exec-log-entry-header" onclick="toggleExecLogEntry('${tabName}', ${idx})">
        ${statusBadge}
        ${triggerBadge}
        <span style="color:#64748b;">${log.executed_at}</span>
        <span style="flex:1; color:#334155;">${summaryText}</span>
        <span style="color:#94a3b8; font-size:10px;">▼ 詳細</span>
      </div>
      <div class="exec-log-entry-body" id="exec-log-entry-body-${tabName}-${idx}">
        ${detailHtml}
      </div>
    </div>`;
}

function buildSummaryText(tabName, summary) {
  if (tabName === 'jidou') {
    if (summary.error_message) return `エラー: ${summary.error_message.substring(0, 60)}`;
    const db = summary.db_type === 'all' ? '全件' : summary.db_type === 'honten' ? '本店CA' : 'PCA';
    return `${db} / 合計${summary.total || 0}件（成功${summary.success || 0} / 要確認${summary.reviews || 0} / エラー${summary.errors || 0}）`;
  } else if (tabName === 'shocho') {
    if (summary.error_message) return `エラー: ${summary.error_message.substring(0, 60)}`;
    return `対象${summary.total_receipts || 0}件 / 照合成功${summary.matched_count || 0}件 / 未照合${summary.unmatched_count || 0}件${summary.ai_ocr_count ? ` / AI-OCR${summary.ai_ocr_count}件` : ''}`;
  } else if (tabName === 'shiharai') {
    if (summary.error_message) return `エラー: ${summary.error_message.substring(0, 60)}`;
    const dateStr = summary.transfer_date ? `${summary.transfer_date.substring(0,4)}-${summary.transfer_date.substring(4,6)}-${summary.transfer_date.substring(6,8)}` : '-';
    return `振込日${dateStr} / ${summary.valid_count || 0}件 / ¥${(summary.total_amount || 0).toLocaleString()}`;
  }
  return JSON.stringify(summary).substring(0, 80);
}

function buildDetailHtml(tabName, detail) {
  if (!detail || Object.keys(detail).length === 0) return '<div style="color:#94a3b8;font-size:11px;">詳細なし</div>';
  if (tabName === 'jidou') {
    const results = detail.results || [];
    if (results.length === 0) return '<div style="color:#94a3b8;font-size:11px;">処理結果なし</div>';
    const rows = results.slice(0, 20).map(r => {
      const sc = r.status === 'success' ? '#15803d' : r.status === 'error' ? '#b91c1c' : r.status === 'review' ? '#b45309' : '#64748b';
      let dealLinks = '';
      if (r.sales_id) dealLinks += `<a href="https://secure.freee.co.jp/deals#deal_id=${r.sales_id}" target="_blank" rel="noopener" style="color:#2563eb;font-size:10px;">売上↗</a> `;
      if (r.purchase_id) dealLinks += `<a href="https://secure.freee.co.jp/deals#deal_id=${r.purchase_id}" target="_blank" rel="noopener" style="color:#2563eb;font-size:10px;">仕入↗</a> `;
      if (r.pca_id) dealLinks += `<a href="https://secure.freee.co.jp/deals#deal_id=${r.pca_id}" target="_blank" rel="noopener" style="color:#2563eb;font-size:10px;">PCA↗</a> `;
      return `<tr><td style="color:${sc};font-weight:700;">${r.status}</td><td>${r.name || '-'}</td><td>${r.action || '-'}</td><td>${(r.message || '').substring(0, 40)} ${dealLinks}</td></tr>`;
    }).join('');
    const more = results.length > 20 ? `<tr><td colspan="4" style="color:#94a3b8;">... 他${results.length - 20}件</td></tr>` : '';
    return `<table class="exec-log-detail-table"><thead><tr><th>ステータス</th><th>名前</th><th>処理</th><th>メッセージ</th></tr></thead><tbody>${rows}${more}</tbody></table>`;
  } else if (tabName === 'shocho') {
    const matched = detail.matched || [];
    const unmatched = detail.unmatched || [];
    const errors = detail.errors || [];
    let html = '';
    if (matched.length > 0) {
      const rows = matched.slice(0, 10).map(m => {
        const dealUrl = m.deal_url || (m.deal_id ? `https://secure.freee.co.jp/deals#deal_id=${m.deal_id}` : '');
        const dealLink = dealUrl ? `<a href="${dealUrl}" target="_blank" rel="noopener" style="color:#2563eb;font-size:10px;">↗</a>` : '';
        return `<tr><td>✅ 照合成功</td><td>${(m.receipt_description || m.receipt_name || m.name || '-').substring(0, 40)}</td><td>${m.deal_partner || '-'} ${dealLink}</td></tr>`;
      }).join('');
      const more = matched.length > 10 ? `<tr><td colspan="3" style="color:#94a3b8;">... 他${matched.length - 10}件</td></tr>` : '';
      html += `<table class="exec-log-detail-table"><thead><tr><th>結果</th><th>書類名</th><th>照合先</th></tr></thead><tbody>${rows}${more}</tbody></table>`;
    }
    if (unmatched.length > 0) {
      html += `<div style="margin-top:6px;color:#b45309;font-size:11px;">未照合: ${unmatched.length}件</div>`;
    }
    if (errors.length > 0) {
      html += `<div style="margin-top:4px;color:#b91c1c;font-size:11px;">エラー: ${errors.slice(0,3).join(', ')}</div>`;
    }
    return html || '<div style="color:#94a3b8;font-size:11px;">詳細なし</div>';
  } else if (tabName === 'shiharai') {
    const targets = detail.targets || [];
    const skipped = detail.skipped || [];
    let html = '';
    if (targets.length > 0) {
      const rows = targets.slice(0, 10).map(t => `<tr><td>${t.partner_name || '-'}</td><td style="text-align:right;">¥${(t.amount || 0).toLocaleString()}</td><td>${t.due_date || '-'}</td></tr>`).join('');
      const more = targets.length > 10 ? `<tr><td colspan="3" style="color:#94a3b8;">... 他${targets.length - 10}件</td></tr>` : '';
      html += `<table class="exec-log-detail-table"><thead><tr><th>取引先</th><th>金額</th><th>決済期日</th></tr></thead><tbody>${rows}${more}</tbody></table>`;
    }
    if (skipped.length > 0) {
      html += `<div style="margin-top:6px;color:#64748b;font-size:11px;">除外: ${skipped.length}件</div>`;
    }
    return html || '<div style="color:#94a3b8;font-size:11px;">詳細なし</div>';
  }
  return `<pre style="font-size:10px;overflow-x:auto;">${JSON.stringify(detail, null, 2).substring(0, 500)}</pre>`;
}

// ===== 仕訳アシスタント：会話セッションログ =====
let _chatSessionLogLoaded = false;

async function loadChatSessionLog(forceReload = false) {
  const contentEl = document.getElementById('exec-log-content-assistant');
  const countEl = document.getElementById('exec-log-count-assistant');
  if (!contentEl) return;
  if (!forceReload && _chatSessionLogLoaded) return;
  try {
    const r = await fetch('/api/chat_sessions');
    const data = await r.json();
    const sessions = data.sessions || [];
    _chatSessionLogLoaded = true;
    if (countEl) countEl.textContent = sessions.length > 0 ? `（${sessions.length}件）` : '';
    if (sessions.length === 0) {
      contentEl.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#94a3b8; font-size:12px; padding:8px 0;">会話履歴なし</div>';
      return;
    }
    contentEl.innerHTML = sessions.map((s, idx) => buildChatSessionEntry(s, idx)).join('');
  } catch(e) {
    if (contentEl) contentEl.innerHTML = `<div style="color:#dc3545; font-size:12px; padding:8px 0;">ログ取得エラー: ${e.message}</div>`;
  }
}

function buildChatSessionEntry(session, idx) {
  const startedAt = session.started_at ? session.started_at.replace('T', ' ').substring(0, 16) : '-';
  const lastAt = session.last_at ? session.last_at.replace('T', ' ').substring(0, 16) : '-';
  const msgCount = session.msg_count || 0;
  const firstMsg = (session.first_user_msg || '').substring(0, 60);
  return `
    <div class="exec-log-entry">
      <div class="exec-log-entry-header" onclick="toggleChatSessionDetail(${idx})" style="cursor:pointer;">
        <span class="exec-log-badge-manual">手動</span>
        <span style="color:#64748b;">${startedAt}</span>
        <span style="flex:1; color:#334155;">${firstMsg || '(発言なし)'}</span>
        <span style="color:#94a3b8; font-size:10px;">メッセージ${msgCount}件 ↓</span>
      </div>
      <div class="exec-log-entry-body" id="chat-session-body-${idx}" style="display:none; padding:8px 12px;">
        <div style="font-size:11px; color:#64748b; margin-bottom:6px;">最終発言: ${lastAt} / セッションID: <code>${session.session_id}</code></div>
        <button class="btn btn-secondary" style="font-size:11px; padding:3px 10px;" onclick="loadAndShowChatSession('${session.session_id}', ${idx})">💬 会話内容を表示</button>
        <div id="chat-session-messages-${idx}" style="margin-top:8px;"></div>
      </div>
    </div>`;
}

function toggleChatSessionDetail(idx) {
  const body = document.getElementById(`chat-session-body-${idx}`);
  if (!body) return;
  body.style.display = body.style.display === 'none' ? 'block' : 'none';
}

async function loadAndShowChatSession(sessionId, idx) {
  const msgEl = document.getElementById(`chat-session-messages-${idx}`);
  if (!msgEl) return;
  msgEl.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#888;font-size:12px;">読み込み中...</div>';
  try {
    const r = await fetch(`/api/chat_history/${sessionId}`);
    const data = await r.json();
    const messages = data.messages || [];
    if (messages.length === 0) {
      msgEl.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#94a3b8;font-size:12px;">メッセージなし</div>';
      return;
    }
    msgEl.innerHTML = messages.map(m => {
      const isUser = m.role === 'user';
      const bg = isUser ? '#eff6ff' : '#f8fafc';
      const label = isUser ? '👤 ユーザー' : '🤖 AI';
      const content = (m.content || '').substring(0, 300).replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;');
      return `<div style="margin-bottom:6px; padding:6px 8px; background:${bg}; border-radius:4px; font-size:11px;"><strong>${label}:</strong> ${content}${m.content && m.content.length > 300 ? '...' : ''}</div>`;
    }).join('');
  } catch(e) {
    msgEl.innerHTML = `<div style="color:#dc3545;font-size:12px;">取得エラー: ${e.message}</div>`;
  }
}

async function registerAiEntries(entries, withFiles = true) {
  const resultDiv = addAiMessage('assistant', '⏳ freeeに登録中...');
  try {
    const res = await fetch('/api/assistant/register_bulk', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ entries })
    });
    const data = await res.json();
    if (data.status === 'ok') {
      const idLinks2 = (data.ids||[]).map(id => `<a href="https://secure.freee.co.jp/deals#deal_id=${id}" target="_blank" rel="noopener" style="color:#2563eb;">${id} ↗</a>`).join(', ');
      let msg = `✅ 登録完了！${data.registered}件をfreeeに登録しました。<br>登録ID: ${idLinks2}`;
      if (withFiles && aiFiles.length > 0 && data.ids && data.ids.length > 0) {
        resultDiv.innerHTML = '⏳ 証憑ファイルをアップロード中...';
        const uploadResult = await uploadReceiptsToDeals(aiFiles, data.ids);
        msg += `<br>📎 証憑: ${uploadResult}`;
        aiFiles = []; renderAiFileList();
      }
      resultDiv.remove(); addAiMessage('assistant', msg);
    } else {
      resultDiv.remove(); addAiMessage('error', `❌ 登録エラー: ${data.message}`);
    }
  } catch(e) { resultDiv.remove(); addAiMessage('error', `❌ 通信エラー: ${e.message}`); }
}
</script>
{% endblock %}

{% block scripts %}
<script>
async function runSingle(pageId, dbType, btn) {
  btn.disabled = true;
  btn.textContent = '処理中...';
  const span = document.getElementById('result-' + pageId);
  try {
    const r = await fetch('/run/single', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},
      body: JSON.stringify({page_id: pageId, db_type: dbType}),
    });
    const data = await r.json();
    if (data.status === 'success') {
      span.style.color = '#28a745';
      span.textContent = '✅ ' + data.message;
      btn.textContent = '✅ 登録済み';
    } else if (data.status === 'review') {
      span.style.color = '#856404';
      span.textContent = '⚠️ ' + data.message;
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = '▶ この1件を登録';
    } else {
      span.style.color = '#dc3545';
      span.textContent = '❌ ' + data.message;
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = '▶ この1件を登録';
    }
  } catch(e) {
    span.style.color = '#dc3545';
    span.textContent = 'エラー: ' + e.message;
    btn.disabled = false;
    btn.textContent = '▶ この1件を登録';
  }
}

async function runAll() {
  const span = document.getElementById('run-all-result');
  span.textContent = '処理中...';
  try {
    const r = await fetch('/run', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},
      body: JSON.stringify({db_type: '{{ db_type }}'}),
    });
    const data = await r.json();
    span.style.color = (data.errors || 0) > 0 ? '#dc3545' : '#28a745';
    span.textContent = `完了: 成功${data.success || 0}件 / 要確認${data.reviews || 0}件 / エラー${data.errors || 0}件`;
    setTimeout(() => location.reload(), 2000);
  } catch(e) {
    span.style.color = '#dc3545';
    span.textContent = 'エラー: ' + e.message;
  }
}
</script>
{% endblock %}

{% block scripts %}
<script>
function toJST(isoStr) {
  if (!isoStr) return '';
  try {
    let s = isoStr;
    if (!s.endsWith('Z') && !s.includes('+') && s.length >= 16) s = s + 'Z';
    const d = new Date(s);
    if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return isoStr.slice(0, 16);
    return d.toLocaleString('ja-JP', {
      timeZone: 'Asia/Tokyo',
      year: 'numeric', month: '2-digit', day: '2-digit',
      hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit'
    });
  } catch(e) { return isoStr.slice(0, 16); }
}
document.querySelectorAll('.ts-cell').forEach(cell => {
  const ts = cell.getAttribute('data-ts');
  if (ts) cell.textContent = toJST(ts);
});
</script>
{% endblock %}
{% endblock %}

{% block scripts %}
<script>
function showTab(id, btn) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.rules-section').forEach(s => s.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.rules-tab-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
  document.getElementById(id).classList.add('active');
  if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
  location.hash = id;
}

// URLハッシュがあれば対応タブを開く
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  const hash = location.hash.replace('#', '');
  if (hash) {
    const target = document.getElementById(hash);
    if (target) {
      document.querySelectorAll('.rules-section').forEach(s => s.classList.remove('active'));
      document.querySelectorAll('.rules-tab-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
      target.classList.add('active');
      // 対応するボタンをアクティブに
      document.querySelectorAll('.rules-tab-btn').forEach(b => {
        if (b.getAttribute('onclick') && b.getAttribute('onclick').includes(hash)) {
          b.classList.add('active');
        }
      });
    }
  }
});
</script>
{% endblock %}
